<ol><li>masculinity

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:manometer.html>manometer</a> (81592)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language"><a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">manomètre</i>, formed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek"><a href = vnd.unilang:ancient.html>Ancient</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:greek.html>Greek</a></a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">μανός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">manós</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:thin.html>thin</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">μέτρον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">métron</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English"><a href = class="Latn mention" lang="es">manto</i>), <a href = vnd.unilang:probably.html>probably</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a lang="cel-gau">*mantalos</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">trodden <a href = class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Celtic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Celtic language">Proto-Celtic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="cel-pro">*mantos</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="cel-pro">*mantlos</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*MenH-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span <hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb"><a href = vnd.unilang:verb.html>Verb</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mantle.html>mantle</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular <a href = vnd.unilang:simple.html>simple</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:present.html>present</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">mantles</b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:present.html>present</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:participle.html>participle</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">mantling</b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:simple.html>simple</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:past.html>past</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:past.html>past</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:participle.html>participle</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">mantled</b>)
</p>

***maren.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:maren.html>maren</a> (21292)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:maren.html>maren</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*māren</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*mērijaną</i>. Cognate <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:high.html>High</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">māren</i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:related.html>Related</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mare.html>mare</a></i>.
